TITLE       Tabulated cross sections for hydrogen and helium      O0289  1    3 
            particles produced by 62 and 29 MeV protons on 120-Sn O0289  1    4 
AUTHOR     (F.E.Bertrand,R.W.Peelle)                              O0289  1    5 
REFERENCE  (R,ORNL-4471,1970)                                     O0289  1    6 
           (J,PR/C,8,1045,1973) Combined paper where the data for O0289  1    7 
           some targets were collected.                           O0289  1    8 
INSTITUTE  (1USAORL)                                              O0289  1    9 
FACILITY   (ISOCY,1USAORL) Oak Ridge Isochronous Cyclotron.       O0289  1   10 
INC-SPECT   Monoenergetic 60.9 - 61.9 +/- 0.1 and 28.8 +/- 0.1 MeVO0289  1   11 
            protons, focused on the target in a spot of approxi-  O0289  1   12 
            mately 8 mm diameter, with a walk of +/- 0.4 cm. The  O0289  1   13 
            uncertainty in number of protons striking the target  O0289  1   14 
            was +/- 1 %.                                          O0289  1   15 
METHOD     (EDE) The secondary particle type was identified with  O0289  1   16 
           (TOF) A combination of delta-E versus E and flight-    O0289  1   17 
            time versus E, which permitted unambiguous            O0289  1   18 
           identification from a few MeV up to 62 MeV. The        O0289  1   19 
           low-energy cutoffs for the different particles were    O0289  1   20 
           ------------------------------------------------------ O0289  1   21 
           61.5 MeV                                               O0289  1   22 
                  Protons               1.8 MeV                   O0289  1   23 
                  Deuterons             4.6 MeV                   O0289  1   24 
                  Tritons               5.7 MeV                   O0289  1   25 
                  Helium-3             13.2 MeV                   O0289  1   26 
                  Alphas               11.0 MeV                   O0289  1   27 
             28.8 MeV                                             O0289  1   28 
                  Protons               1.9 MeV                   O0289  1   29 
                  Deuterons             4.6 MeV                   O0289  1   30 
                  Tritons               5.7 MeV                   O0289  1   31 
                  Helium-3             13.2 MeV                   O0289  1   32 
                  Alphas               11.0 MeV                   O0289  1   33 
           ------------------------------------------------------ O0289  1   34 
DETECTOR   (TELES,SI,GELI) A solid state three-detector           O0289  1   35 
           telescope, with two silicon delta-E detectors and a    O0289  1   36 
            lithium-drifted germanium detector used for total     O0289  1   37 
            energy absorption. The delta-E detectors had          O0289  1   38 
           thicknesses of 100 and 500 um.                         O0289  1   39 
           The telescope was mounted in a scattering chamber with O0289  1   40 
           1.2 m diameter.                                        O0289  1   41 
            The total resolution was approximately 180 keV for    O0289  1   42 
            most of the data. The telescope was shielded by       O0289  1   43 
           tantalum or nickel collimators. For the 61.5 MeV runs  O0289  1   44 
            the tantalum collimator had a thickness of 0.432 cm   O0289  1   45 
            and an area of 0.522 cm2. The two nickel collimators  O0289  1   46 
            had a thickness of 0.653 cm and areas of 0.183 and    O0289  1   47 
            0.265 cm2, respectively. For the 28.8 MeV runs, a     O0289  1   48 
            0.013 cm thick tantalum collimator, with an area of   O0289  1   49 
            o.522 cm2, was used. The uncertainty in the           O0289  1   50 
           collimator areas was +/- 1.5 %.                        O0289  1   51 
           The distance from the target to the collimator was     O0289  1   52 
            around 46 cm +/- 1%.                                  O0289  1   53 
           The collimators had a misalignment at the center of theO0289  1   54 
           scattering chamber of +/- 0.5 cm. The precision of the O0289  1   55 
           detector angle was +/- 0.5 degrees.                    O0289  1   56 
           The zero angle was determined to +/- 0.5 degrees.      O0289  1   57 
           The angular resolution was +/- 1.2 degrees.            O0289  1   58 
SAMPLE     Tin target, 4.85 +/- 0.05 mg/cm2 thick, with a         O0289  1   59 
           thickness nonuniformity of +/- 1%.  The isotopic       O0289  1   60 
           composition was 98.4% 120-Sn, 0.5% 118-Sn, 0.4%        O0289  1   61 
           119-Sn, 0.3% 124-Sn and 0.4% other.                    O0289  1   62 
           The sample had a small contaminant of nickel and       O0289  1   63 
           oxygen.   The sample was oriented with an angular      O0289  1   64 
           precision of +/- 0.5 degrees.                          O0289  1   65 
CORRECTION .The Data were corrected for                           O0289  1   66 
            1. Energy loss of the secondary particles in the      O0289  1   67 
               target,                                            O0289  1   68 
            2. Collimator edge penetration,                       O0289  1   69 
            3. Multiple scattering of particles in the first two  O0289  1   70 
           detectors, which made them miss the total absorption   O0289  1   71 
           detector,                                              O0289  1   72 
            4. The nickel window dead layer of the Ge-detector,   O0289  1   73 
               and,                                               O0289  1   74 
            5. Nuclear reactions in the Ge-detector.              O0289  1   75 
ERR-ANALYS (ERR-S) Statistical error in Data.                     O0289  1   76 
           (ERR-1) Systematic error in Data, with contributions   O0289  1   77 
            such as                                               O0289  1   78 
            1. Uncertainty in various corrections  +/- 2 %.       O0289  1   79 
            2. Uncertainty in number of protons                   O0289  1   80 
               striking the target                 +/- 1 %.       O0289  1   81 
            3. Uncertainty in dead time            +/- 2 %.       O0289  1   82
